<Author>alamosf
<Content>nice hotel, sketchy location Stayed at the Raco del Pi for six nights in December and while I thought the hotel itself was very well-managed (spotless rooms and responsive staff) and the amenities, especially the free in-room internet hookup since I'd brought my laptop, were excellent, I agree with a previous post which mentioned that the hotel's location leaves much to be desired. While the hotel is right smack in the center of the action, especially for the daily evening 'paseo' (the stroll that most Europeans take at dusk), I would prefer to join this daily ritual at will and not be subjected to injecting myself into a mass of people each time I leave the hotel. I consider myself a somewhat experienced traveler, having been all over Asia and Europe doing the 'backpacker' thing, and now that I'm perhaps a little older and a bit more cautious, I would have preferred something a bit more quiet and further away from the 'action'. Yes, there is a sex shop next door and many tacky shops in the immediate vicinity. If ever I do go back to Barcelona, I'd choose to stay in the adjacent Eixample neighborhood which has wide boulevards and a reasonable amount of commercial activity and establishments (banks, restaurants, shops), enough to reassure visitors of 'being' in Barcelona without having to deal with the tackier side of it all. And don't worry - the Barri Gotic is just an interesting 10-minute walk away.

<Author>sklo2004
<Content>Nice clean rooms, great location, impeccable service, and delicious breakfast! You really cannot find a hotel that is more centrally located than H10 Raco del Pi. It is 2 blocks away from Las Ramblas, right in the middle of Barri Gotic's excitement. There are countless shops (from antique, clothing, art, to accessories), restaurants, cafes, and beautiful landmarks within 50 footsteps. If you are looking for a real taste of Gothic Quarters energy and spirit, this is the ideal place to stay. It's a very exciting and active location. If you can, ask for a window that oversees the Gothic Quarters. It may be loud (so don't do that if you want peace and quiet), but it allows you to soak in the environment.The room itself is clean and spacious. Furnishing is modern and simple- not elegant but is comfortable. The front desk staff is so consistenly friendly and helpful. The free daily breakfast buffet was delicious. It wasn't just continental, they served sausages, eggs, fresh fruits, muffins, cheese plates and cure meat plates. I thought it was refreshing to have normal sausage and eggs again after 10 days of jamon iberica everywhere I went for breakfast. Coffee, tea and snack service is complimentary all day until 8pm. And even better, you get free Internet access too, although there is only one computer to serve the 20+ rooms of guests.I stayed in 2 different hotels while in Barcelona just to try out different areas. Avenida Palace, the other hotel I stayed at, although more opulent and elegant in decor, cannot compare to H10's service and location.

<Author>Mark235
<Content>Could not find better location I stayed in H10 Raco Del Pi between January 14 and 16. Great hotel. I have never been before to Barcelona and choose this hotel because of the previous review on Trip Advisor. I was not disappointed. The location is exceptional, about 1 minute walk from the Gothic Cathedral and 1 minute walk from Las Remblas. Despite the proximity of Las Remblas, the location is very safe (I walked in the Gothic quarter at around 1:30 a.m. and never felt threatened). Staff is helpful, though contrary to other review I was not welcomed with Cava.I did not pay 14 euros for the breakfast and found out that it was a good idea. There are plenty of cafes around the hotel where you can get breakfast for between 2 euros and 5 euros; for instance, on plaza del pi, just across the hotel, I got for 3.8 eurosa glass of freshly-pressed orange juice, a chocolate croissant and a milk coffee.Rooms are well-furnished and very clean. However, do not expect your room to have a great view, since the hotel is in a side street in the gothic quarter. The rooms with the best view are the ones located on the face of the street; all other rooms face walls of adjacent buildings. But this is really the only small disagreement one can find in this hotel.Finally, on an unrelated note, please be aware that some restaurants use their on conversion rates when you pay your meal with foreign credit cards. This happened to me in a restaurant just across the Sagrada Familia. I paid with a Canadian card and on my receipt there was a note specifying that I had accepted not to get Mastercard international conversion rate (2.5%) but rather the restaurant conversion rate (12% !!!). I was alone and did not spend much, but still it was an unpleasant surprise.

Our room was not a large as some hotel rooms but it was very clean, smart and a lovely bathroom with lots of complimentary toiletries. Bed was hard but that was ideal for me, just to warn people who dont like hard beds.There is a little area downstairs which have self service coffee and pastries, this was great as after a long walk we would go to the hotel rather than a coffee shop for coffee, great coffee to. The internet corner is also very helpful.The location is perfect, about two minutes from the ramblas and cathedral, we walked everywhere. We took a bus from right outside the airport (3.60 euro single) which took us to Catalunya plaza and it was a 5 to 10 minute walk to the hotel if you dont want to cab, its also easy to find.We didnt have the breakfast so cant comment on food, but there are lots of little cafes nearby where we took breakfast.The place is fab, great location, great staff, great price.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>What a terrific hotel! Stayed here for 3 nights from 31st Oct. 2005. Having read the reviews on TripAdvisor before we went we were expecting a good hotel but it was even more than we could have hoped for. Location is outstanding. It is a few hundreds yards from Las Ramblas in the Barrio Gothica, and yet the street is extremely quiet at night. Some of the narrow, quieter streets can be somewhat intimidating and look at bit dodgy after 10pm but Del Pi is well lit and safe, with a beautiful square of the same name.It is very easy to get to from the airport by train to the Sants-Estacio and from here you can switch to the Metro Green line heading for Canyelles. This will bring you to Liceu metro station which is 2 minutes walk from the hotel.You will be greeted with your complimentary glass of champagne while being checked in by the very efficient, pleasant and helpful staff. Rooms were spotless and very comfortable with a modern bathroom and a huge range of toiletries. There is definitely no need for a bigger room in Barcelona as you are out and about so much. Breakfast was a feast. As well as a huge selection of juices, fresh fruit, meats, cheese, fresh rolls, croissants, bacon, sausages and scrambled eggs, you could have baked cheesecake, chocolate fudge cake, apple tart and a range of other cakes catering for your sweet tooth!! Cakes and croissants were available free throughout the rest of the day, as was tea and coffee. (This may explain why scales were provided in the bathroom!)The glass of champagne as we were checking out was just a perfect end to our trip. This hotel is a little gem, in a street with a lot of character. We will definitely be going back.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Perfect location in a tourist hot spot The H10 hotel Raco del pi is ideally located for those who want to be in the center of barcelona's tourist area, la ramblas. While the rooms are just average for the price the hotel's main asset is the free food and drinks that are available to all guests. The only downside was that the non-smoking rooms smelled smoky at times when other guests were smoking. <Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Great Hotel The hotel was excellent. The free champagne at check-in. The room. The breakfast. The mineral water and soft drinks and peanuts at the outdoor patio. One thing that I did appreciate was the written safety material provided at check-in. The woman at the check-in desk made a point of saying, It is unfortunate that we have a problem with theft here in Barcelona. Here is some written material about safety precautions. Please read it. I had never had someone say that and, quite frankly, it spooked me a little bit. I did, however, read the material when I got to my room. Mostly common sense suggestions, though my sensitivity was heigntened. One thing that was emphasized was the fact that theft was partuicularly rampant near the central railway station.I broke-up my trip in Barcelona with a few days in Palma. When I returned from the airport to the central railway station, I noticed a few guys who seemed shady. The pushed their way between me and my wife on the escalator up to the street and when I got to the top the guy in front of me bent over as though he had dropped something to block my way. The two guys behind me were about to press up against me to pick my pockets, no doubt. I immediately realized what was going on so I dropped my shoulder and reverted back to the offensive lineman on my high school football team and I barrelled-over the guy who was attempting to block my way. I managed to hold onto my bags and I let out quite a few obcenities--in English--to the puzzled guys who feigned surprise. They got nothing.Interesting to note that two English girls sitting at an adjacent table at an outdoor cafe were approached by a nice young man and after he left one girl's wallet was gone. Be careful in Barcelona. Theft is rampant! You might want to consider having a decoy wallet: an old wallet filled with expired credit cards and a wad of worthless cash (e.g., 100,000 old Romanian lei or Bulgarian leva). If someone goes for your wallet they will get the decoy wallet and promptly walk away to examine their (worthless) booty. Ha, ha, ha, ha, ha.

<Author>ShowMeState
<Content>Great Stay at H10 Raco Del Pi Just returned from a 3 night stay at the Raco Del Pi. The hotel room, staff, and location was great. I was a little nervous before arrival about staying close to Las Ramblas, but, the hotel location is perfect. It is close enough to the hub of Barcelona, but, it is located on a side street that is quiet at night.The hotel staff members went out of their way to assist us with directions. They were the most professional of the three other hotels we stayed in on this trip.Be aware that taxis are not allowed on the street where the hotel is situated. They have to drop you off at the entrance of the street. The hotel is just a short walk, but, it can be a little disconcerting when the taxi driver tells you to get out.I highly recommend this hotel and Barcelona. The shopping and the architecture in Barcelolna was great. It was also quite a bargain compared to prices in Brussels and Paris which were our next two stops.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Fab location We researched quite a bit on which area of Barcelona we wanted to stay in. We wanted a hotel that was in easy reach of La Rambla, the beach, and the nightlife. The Raco Del Pi was perfect for location. We were surrounded by so many clothes and shoe shops (much to by husbands horror) and there was plenty of small spanish bars around to have a drink in. The area seemed to be buzzing all day (especially on saturday). The 1st room that we were given was small, so we moved to room 208 which was a much better size. That was the only down side to the hotel. The rooms are very clean and newly decorated. When you arrive you get a glass of Cava which is a nice touch. In the bar you can have tea, coffee, water,croissants  pain au chocolate which are free for the duration of your stay, this saved us on buying breakfast every day. There is also a computer which has free internet access - great for checking out the weather on. We will definetely stay at the H10 Raco Del Pi again when we go back to Barcelona.

<Author>rdcocker
<Content>Not all it seems When my fiance and I first got to the hotel we were greeted with complementary glasses of sparkling wine. This was just what we needed after an arduous journey from girona airport some 40 miles north of Barcelona. After this, we were shown to our room by the porter who carried our luggage and left us to examine our surroundings. The room was of a contemporary style with a laminate wooden floor and brand-new furniture, and everything was spotless. We were suitably impressed!! The main problem we had however, was that because we were staying on the top floor our window was at floor level and was tiny. On closer inspection there was a thick concrete grid infront of the window, doubtless to prevent hapless toddlers from tumbling to an unpleasant and certain death below. This gave a distinct claustrophobic feeling to the room and in daytime hours the room was virtually pitch-black!! The bathroom was equally contemporary; quite basic but tastefully decorated. However, if you like taking a bath instead of a shower, you will have a problem.... unless you happen to be 3 feet tall!The breakfast service is very good. I have to admit that of all the BBs I have been to, this is one of the best. The dining room is very comfortable and modern, and the choice of food is good. You can get your full English (except for the sausages which are never as good abroad), continental, cereals and a whole host of fruit. The quality of the food is good as well. Often, otherwise decent BBs really let themselves down by serving up stale bread buns and rock-hard croissants. The food here seems very fresh indeed. Another good point is that breakfast is served till about 10.30, much later than most.The location is what I was primarily interested in when I booked this hotel. Its located on a little side-street just off the infamous Las Ramblas, which is extremely popular with Barcelona tourists. The hotel is nearer the north end of Las Ramblas, further away from the harbour than other hotels I was considering. THIS WAS A VERY GOOD THING, because at around dusk, the nearer you progress towards the harbour, the more decidedly dodgey Las Ramblas and its side-streets become. I had heard this before I came here, but did not believe it......believe me...its true!!So far, so good! Why have I rated this hotel as just OK? No doubt our stay at the hotel was pleasant, and we had a great time in Barcelona. I rate this hotel as just 'OK' because their after-sale service was appalling!! I had the misfortune of leaving my wallet in a taxi from Raco Del Pi to the coach station. This was entirely my fault. I noticed this straight after being dropped off by the taxi, and called the hotel who had booked the taxi so that they may inform the driver. They fobbed me off and didn't even attempt to contact the driver. When I finally got back to the UK I called them again and they told me it was my fault (which I admit, it was) and they could not help. I emailed them again and again. They wouldn't even tell me which taxi company it was that they used (even though they knew which one it was). I know its unlikely I would ever have seen my wallet again, but their attitude stunk. Not only were they unhelpful, but they were positively rude. They'd got my money, so why should they care? This completely soured my feeling towards the company and I will not return to them.So, if you don't intend needing their services in the event of a minor crisis once you have parted with your hard earned cash, this is actually a rather good place to stay in Barcelona. But, be warned!! If you ever require anything which isn't obliged of them as a result of paying to stay in their hotel........you get the message!  
<Date>Apr 19, 2005

<Author>croakey
<Content>Great hotel, great location, great service Recently returned from short break, staying in the Raco del Pi. Location is brilliant; rooms, lobby, restaurant all spotlessly clean, everyone working at the hotel really friendly and couldn't do enough for you. Just be aware that if you get a room overlooking the street outside, the rubbish collection (that means the streets are also litter free) happens in the early hours of the morning so use that as an excuse to stay out even later than you'd planned - the area around the hotel seemed quite safe and trouble free, even very late.

<Author>Nell59
<Content>Excellent hotel Excellent Location After a lot of consideration and checking reviews of 3* hotels on this web site, we decided on the Raco del Pi. We were so pleased with our choice, this is a really good small friendly hotel with excellent staff and in an excellent location.Got a really good deal from last minute.com - 62 a night b/b. After reading some of the reviews we requested a large lower floor room with windows! we got a lovely large room on the second floor (202) with a large bathroom with a jaccuzi bath. However it did face the front and if you like to have a 'siesta' you may have trouble sleeping as a boutique across the road had music playing all day.But we did not find it noisy at night (maybe different in the summer months)unfortunately we picked the week Barcelona had freezing cold weather but we braved sitting on top of the tour bus taking in all the beauty of this city. Highlights for us were discovering all the narrow streets and squares of the gothic area and Parc Guell.Would definately stay at this Hotel again.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Spotless, friendly  Thanks to this website and reviews we found the Hotel Raco Del Pi. We were not disappointed. The hotel is on a side street from La Ramblas in one of the nicer parts of the Barra Gothic. The hotel itself is spotless with modern decor and a great breakfast buffet. Rooms are spacious although a little dark but that would be my only criticism. The staff are friendly and very helpful. The hotel is a 5 min short walk from the Catalunya metro station and so transfering from the airport is easy. It is at the more expensive end of the market but I think it is worth paying the extra money. Some parts of the Gothic quarter (like other major cities) can be a bit dingy and have streets that I wouldn't want to walk down at night. This was not the case with the Raco del Pi the street is well lit, fairly busy with evening walkers and was well away from the (as the guide books puts it) dodgy end of town. Overall a great hotel, good value for money  great location. For a short break it's perfect.   
<Date>May 27, 2004

<Author>Doc_Jon
<Content>Nice, but dark room We really liked this hotel. The location was excellent, near to La Rambla and all the sites of the Gothic quarter. The hotel itself was very clean and modern, the service was very good. The only disadvantage was our room (no. 105). It was quite small and only had 1 window which looked onto a brick wall. We could barely see the sky. As a consequence, there was not much natural light and so we had to have the lights on at all times. The facilities, however, were very good in the room. We particularly liked the radio built into the headboard. There was also a good range of digital channels. The minibar was reasonably priced, 1.75 euros for a bottle of water. All in all, we enjoyed our stay at the hotel, but if staying for more than one night, we would have asked for a different room.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>We loved the raco del pi We stayed at the Raco del Pi for 3 nights in a suprisingly cold spell in February. We liked it straight away. It is in the narrow lanes of the Gothic Quarter. The taxi couldn't get in to drop us off so we had a short walk from the Ramblas. A nice glasss of bubbly awaited us in reception, a nice touch. Everything is walkable and we felt we got the most out of our short stay by being in a central location. The hotel staff are friendly and the rooms are well appointed, very clean, modern and spacious. The hotel is very cosy compared to larger more gltzy places. Good value for money. We didn't eat in the restaurant because there is so much choice nearby. We would certainly stay there again.
